  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

  <span id="freeText9661633782307315919" style="display:none"><i> “Rainelle, you were eye-f***ing me in the casino.” </i> <br /> <br />Rae couldn't exactly deny what Andrei, the king of the incubi, said so matter-of-factly.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1327801129" />
    <a title="Talltree" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1869868-talltree"><img alt="Talltree" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579433935p2/1869868.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1327801129?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Talltree" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Talltree" href="/user/show/1869868-talltree">Talltree</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/24906900-how-to-kill-an-incubus">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1869868-talltree?shelf=fav-non-contemp">fav-non-contemp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1869868-talltree?shelf=genre-pnr-uf">genre-pnr-uf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1327801129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8084391712094013985">Smutty and fun UF romance between PI h who specialises in cheating husbands and a demon king who is an incubus. h turns out to be H's fated mate(kind of) and theres loads of hot (and rough) smex! <br/>There are some obstacles to the HEA too but I liked that the h/H weren't among them. In almost all UF stories the h is kickass but emotionally stunted and puts up every objection on earth - and some more - to distance herself from the H. Or she chooses some emotionally unavailable, manipulative jerk out</span>
  <span id="freeText8084391712094013985" style="display:none">Smutty and fun UF romance between PI h who specialises in cheating husbands and a demon king who is an incubus. h turns out to be H's fated mate(kind of) and theres loads of hot (and rough) smex! <br />There are some obstacles to the HEA too but I liked that the h/H weren't among them. In almost all UF stories the h is kickass but emotionally stunted and puts up every objection on earth - and some more - to distance herself from the H. Or she chooses some emotionally unavailable, manipulative jerk out of all the choices available to her. Luckily in this one while h and H are wary and take some time to fall completely for each other, there is no angst and the obstacles are from outside forces. The h was adorably funny and snarky and sweet at times and the H was stalkerisly obsessive/possessive. <br /><br />The cliffy ending was disappointing but in a way I was glad I'd be getting more of Rae and Andrei! Hope bk2 will be out soon!!<br /><br />4.75 stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8084391712094013985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1988277140093837364">4.5 Stars.<br/><br/>This book is awesome, but it also has a lot of sizzling hot sex in it too. Some of my friends here might not like this book due to the amount of sex that it has in it and some of the questionable sex. <br/><br/>We are dealing with demons, particularly sex demons. So Rae (Rainelle, interesting name) is a PI, who only does cheating husbands. She lives a pretty mundane life until she wakes up to a demon trying to get in her pants, but he seems off, maybe drunk who knows. She fends him off, and he m</span>
  <span id="freeText1988277140093837364" style="display:none">4.5 Stars.<br /><br />This book is awesome, but it also has a lot of sizzling hot sex in it too. Some of my friends here might not like this book due to the amount of sex that it has in it and some of the questionable sex. <br /><br />We are dealing with demons, particularly sex demons. So Rae (Rainelle, interesting name) is a PI, who only does cheating husbands. She lives a pretty mundane life until she wakes up to a demon trying to get in her pants, but he seems off, maybe drunk who knows. She fends him off, and he mentions that Andrei would really like her because she's his type. Moving forward Rae takes a case that leads her to Vegas and a very hunky guy. She has eye contact with him and later he comes into her room and basically bangs the crazy out of her. Now here is where someone would have issues, Rae doesn't know who he is or what his name is, she still lets him in her pants. I don't have a problem with it and found it pretty sizzling. As we progress in the story we learn that the man she just banged is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Andrei<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[basically the demon king <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and it's surprising then we learn more about Rae's past and her family history as well.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this book but there were some questionable moments particularly with a scene in which <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Andrei was mad(?) at her and basically makes her have sex with him in front of some of his demon people. He was angry I forget what about but he banged her and told her she couldn't climax. He was rough and it was hurtful to Rae. I didn't understand this scene unless it was to make Andrei less nice, since he'd been pretty pleasant prior. But this kind of detracted the warm fuzzies for me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> then there are some other questionable moments that I didn't completely get, but still. The book had plenty of sex and plot to appease me in my most book slump feelings. The pacing is great, the H is someone you're not sure if you like, which for me I enjoy rooting for those kinds of characters. Examples like Damon Salvatore and Klaus Mikaelson come to mind of characters that you love and hate. Yep Andrei is just like that. <br /><br />The ending of the book has me dying for the next one. I'm not sure where it is as it's not showing up on Goodreads, is there a second book? When will there be a second book? I kinda need it NOW! That's how good I felt this book was.</span>

<div id="review_1302793257" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1302793257" />
    <a title="Taffy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26762278-taffy"><img alt="Taffy" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1302793257?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taffy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taffy" href="/user/show/26762278-taffy">Taffy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302793257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer474081013239617596">I have been following Kim for almost two years now in Wattpad. I have read a lot of wattpad stories but I have a short list of authors who I can definitely say are amazing writers and Kim is one of those. I have read all of her works in Wattpad but How to Kill an Incubus is one of my favorites. It's rare for me to like supernatural romances because I can't quite imagine some for reason. This book, though, has surpassed all my expectations. Yes, it is based on a supernatural creature and yet ever</span>
  <span id="freeText474081013239617596" style="display:none">I have been following Kim for almost two years now in Wattpad. I have read a lot of wattpad stories but I have a short list of authors who I can definitely say are amazing writers and Kim is one of those. I have read all of her works in Wattpad but How to Kill an Incubus is one of my favorites. It's rare for me to like supernatural romances because I can't quite imagine some for reason. This book, though, has surpassed all my expectations. Yes, it is based on a supernatural creature and yet every single event on the story seems real. Andrei is more human than incubus for me which makes him relatable rather than a figment of the imagination. It's a fun read. There's enough emotions to last til the end of the story and it keeps you wanting for more. Since I have read this on Wattpad, I would seriously grow anxious waiting for the next chapters but Kim does not disappoint. Every chapter is exciting and fun and at times scary but all in all, a very good read. Most people who've read this hated Rae for quite I well. I like her. I like how mixed up her emotions have been. It makes her relatable and understandable too. I like that she does not back down from Andrei, that she keeps him on his toes but I also like how she needs him and how they both affect each other. It's not anti-feminist to be needy once in a while so she's okay in my book. <br /><br />I'm happy for Kim that she is able to publish this book and I can't wait for her other books to be published. She's that good. And this book, it's that good so I give it 5 stars! Great job Kim!</span>
  <a data-text-id="474081013239617596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13547037243602024681" style="display:none">Kimber Lee is honestly one of my all-time favorite authors. Shortly after first joining Wattpad, I stumbled upon her page, and her dreamy-yet-realistic romance novels captivated me. I've read just about all of her works on the site, and Kim's writing style is the best! I quite literally SQUEAL when I get an update notification from her. <br /><br />She will have you actually laughing out loud at the most random lines, and each character is so unique and complex for every new and original storyline. I personally love it when she writes of badass "Ain't No Wifey"-esque female characters getting paired with swoon-worthy, truly caring yet Very-rough-around-the-edges guys.<br /><br />WARNING: you will get *completely* sucked into her stories. And her male leads set the bar very high. I don't know, call me a hopeless romantic, but Kimber Lee is the master of the erotic-romance-comedy-etc. genre in my eyes. <br /><br />Sorry I'm not doing very well with my words right now, but please try out How to Kill an Incubus!!! I have a strong feeling that you will NOT be disappointed, :)! and CONGRATS KIM, so happy for you and your book getting published YAYYYY &lt;3</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1798064968362211377">Literally, if you enjoy a good drama and a similar level of erotica like Sylvia Day - This is the book for you ! Thoroughly enjoyed every single page.A non-cliche and great story plot, that also exceeded beyond unimaginable erotica. Kimber Lee takes you throughout the journey of the also non-cliche protagonist Rae, with words that will make you both empathetic and sympathetic. In a good freaking good way. <br/><br/>And Andre(drool)(slurps)There are literally no words. Just read it and you'll understand wh</span>
  <span id="freeText1798064968362211377" style="display:none">Literally, if you enjoy a good drama and a similar level of erotica like Sylvia Day - This is the book for you ! Thoroughly enjoyed every single page.A non-cliche and great story plot, that also exceeded beyond unimaginable erotica. Kimber Lee takes you throughout the journey of the also non-cliche protagonist Rae, with words that will make you both empathetic and sympathetic. In a good freaking good way. <br /><br />And Andre(drool)(slurps)There are literally no words. Just read it and you'll understand why.<br /><br />Did I mention Andrei?<br /><br />Ugghh. I could write a whole story of how freaking awesome this story is. Just know that once you start reading, your going to thank me for writing this review and kiss Kimber Lees feet for writing it. Lol.<br /><br />So, what are you waiting for?(besides the publish date on June 21st) <br />KEEP THIS BOOK ON WATCH UNTIL JUNE 21ST ! THEN READ IT !<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2067512679811826037">A supernatural 50 Shades of Grey. & no it's not a compliment.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473164725ra/20419327.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't even know why I even tried to finish this book. The whole thing was just a painful read from the start. The writing was bad, the characters sucked & the plot was just terrible. & let's not even at the horrible cliffhanger for the next book. <br/><br/>Honestly though, if you're looking for a incubi/succubi romance series, you're better off reading the Georgina Kincaid series by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/137902.Richelle_Mead' title='Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Richelle Mead</a> or the Succubus Diaries by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2923539.Jill_Myles' title='Jill Myles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jill Myles</a> instead.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4751066466503937425">I read this book on Wattpad as she was writing it, before she took most of it down due to copyright. It is AMAZING. It's well-written, has complex characters and a good storyline. Andrei is the bad boy- type character and Rainelle is the person stuck between two ideologies (her hunter father's/ Andrei's or (spoiler) Temp's). It is for a mature audience though; however, the sex/mature parts balance out perfectly with the plot and romance between Rainelle and Andrei. It's a must- read if you like </span>
  <span id="freeText4751066466503937425" style="display:none">I read this book on Wattpad as she was writing it, before she took most of it down due to copyright. It is AMAZING. It's well-written, has complex characters and a good storyline. Andrei is the bad boy- type character and Rainelle is the person stuck between two ideologies (her hunter father's/ Andrei's or (spoiler) Temp's). It is for a mature audience though; however, the sex/mature parts balance out perfectly with the plot and romance between Rainelle and Andrei. It's a must- read if you like paranormal/fantasy and romance (with a bit of mature). After you read it, I advise you go the Wattpad and read her other novels that are also very good. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer644803080361007705">I've read everything by Kimber Lee and love her stories. I waited to read How to Kill an Incubus because I'm typically not a fan of paranormal themes. Her story lines are great, her characters well developed and dang if I don't want the man in each story to be my husband! Kimber Lee is very talented and I wish her co</span>
  <span id="freeText644803080361007705" style="display:none">I've read everything by Kimber Lee and love her stories. I waited to read How to Kill an Incubus because I'm typically not a fan of paranormal themes. Was I ever wrong to doubt I wouldn't love this book! I'm impatiently waiting for the book to be released in its entirety. Definitely read this book and anything else by this author. Her story lines are great, her characters well developed and dang if I don't want the man in each story to be my husband! Kimber Lee is very talented and I wish her continued success and lots of new stories for me to read (and re-read). </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8umf+rVhwN8KTvbWogppyt6p6qnUib7C9vqPx/DoRRF6hePg1nmebrWBA4lSSioqCtDwOkzDfl91WnfZGcR5RQ==')})
    }
  }

  }
